)@@G@@   *******  @H@@@F. ******* PRINT (P)          - PRINT NEXT 'M' IMAGES (XT
)@@G@@PRINT M)       *******  @H@F@E. ******* SKIP (S)           - SKIP REST OXU

)@@G@@*** SKIP (S)           - SKIP REST OF INPUT                    *******  XY
)@@G@@@H@@@F. ******* TOP (T)            - GO TO TOP (STARTS SCAN OVER)       XZ

)@@G@@  . IS COPY$ ON?  @E@@@E          J         CONT6             . YES, JUSFY

)@@G@@5     @[@@@E.     @C@@@E.                   IMAGE IS A CONTROL IMAGE    GF

)@@G@@RS IN IMAGE @E@@@F          MSI       A1,FACT,X3        . A1=# CHARS IN PR

)@@G@@FINDFIELD   @E@@@E          J         ERR6              . STRING NOT FOUPT
)@@G@@ND    @D@F@E          SSL       A0,18             . SAVE CHAR PT  @E@@@EPU
)@@G@@          S         A0,A3             . A3=PT INTO IMAGE    @ @@@E      PV
)@@G@@    AU        A1,NTO    @ @@@E          AN        A2,NFROM  @E@F@E      PW
)@@G@@    S         A2,A6             . A6=# CHARS IN AIMAGE@E@@@F          S PX
)@@G@@        A2,A6             . A6=# CHARS IN TEMP  @H@@@E          L,U     PY
)@@G@@  X1,IMAGE          . MOVE 1ST PART OF IMAGE TO ALT IMAGE   @ @F@E      PZ
)@@G@@    L,U       X2,AIMAGE @ @@@F          L,U       X2,TEMP   @ @@@E      QA
)@@G@@    LMJ       X11,BMOVE @ @@@E          LXI       X2,A3     @G@@@E      QB
)@@G@@    L,U       X1,TO             . MOVE 'TO' IMAGE TO ALT IMAGE    @ @@@EQC
)@@G@@          L         A0,NTO    @ @@@F          SZ        BASCII    @ @@@EQD
)@@G@@          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @ @@@E          AU        A3,A0     @ @@@EQE
)@@G@@          LXI       X2,A4     @G@@@E          A         A3,NFROM        QF
)@@G@@  . MOVE REST OF IMAGE TO ALT IMAGE @ @@@E          L,U       X1,IMAGE  QG
)@@G@@@ @@@E          LXI       X1,A3     @ @@@E          L         A0,A1     QH
)@@G@@@ @@@E          AN        A0,A3     @^@@@E          A,U       A0,1@ @@@FQI
)@@G@@          S,H1      X3,BASCII @ @@@E          LMJ       X11,BMOVE @H@F@EQJ
)@@G@@          L         A1,ASCII          . CALC. # OF WORDS IN UPDATED IMAGQK
)@@G@@E     @H@@@F          SZ        A2                . CALC. # OF WORDS IN QL
)@@G@@UPDATED IMAGE     @^@F@E          SZ        A2  @ @@@E          L       QM
)@@G@@  A3,A6     @ @F@E          DI        A2,FACT,A1@ @@@F          DI      QN
)@@G@@  A2,FACT,X3@^@@@E          TZ        A3  @^@@@E          A,U       A2,1QO
)@@G@@@F@@@E          S,S2      A2,CONTROL        . STORE IN CONTROL WORD     QP
)@@G@@@E@F@E          AN,U      A2,1              . BLANK OUT OLD IMAGE @E@@@FQQ
)@@G@@          S         X3,BASCII         . BLANK OUT OLD IMAGE @ @@@F      QR
)@@G@@    L,U       X1,IMAGE  @ @@@F          L         A0,A6     @^@@@F      QS
)@@G@@    A,U       A0,6@ @@@F          LMJ       X11,BBLANK@A@F@E          L QT
)@@G@@        A3,('      ')   @ @F@E          TZ        ASCII     @B@F@E      QU
)@@G@@    L         A3,($CAS('    '))     @A@F@E          S         A3,IMAGE,AQV
)@@G@@2     @ @F@E          JGD       A2,$-1    @G@F@E          L,U       X1,AQW
)@@G@@IMAGE         . MOVE ALT IMAGE BACK TO ORIGINAL @G@@@F          L,U     QX
)@@G@@  X1,TEMP           . MOVE ALT IMAGE BACK TO ORIGINAL @ @@@E          L,QY
)@@G@@U       X2,IMAGE  @ @@@E          L         A0,A6     @ @@@E          LMQZ
)@@G@@J       X11,BMOVE @E@@@E          SLJ       PIMAGE            . PRINT UPRA
)@@G@@DATE IMAGE  @F@@@E          J         READ+1            . READ NEXT USERRB
)@@G@@ COMMAND    @G@@@FFIND      L,U       X3,FINDKEY        . POINT TO POINTRC
)@@G@@ TO FIND DATA     @ @@@F          L,U       X4,NFIMAGE@F@@@FFINDC1    L RD
)@@G@@        A6,CREAD          . BYTE # OF END OF INPUT    @F@@@FFINDL     ANRE
)@@G@@,U      A6,1              . FIND LAST NON-BLANK CHAR  @ @@@F          LXRF
)@@G@@I       X1,A6     @ @@@F          LMJ       X11,BGET  @ @@@F          TNRG
)@@G@@E,U     A0,' '    @ @@@F          J         FINDL     @F@@@F          JNRH
)@@G@@Z       A6,FINDC2         . IS A STRING SPECIFIED?    @H@@@F          TNRI
)@@G@@Z       0,X4              . NO, WAS THERE A PREVIOUS COMMAND?     @F@@@FRJ
)@@G@@          J         ERR7              . NO, INCOMPLETE COMMAND    @F@@@FRK
)@@G@@          SP1       0,X3              . YES, SET FIND/LOCATE KEY  @F@@@FRL
)@@G@@          J         *READ             . REPEAT PREVIOUS COMMAND   @G@@@FRM
)@@G@@FINDC2    AN        A6,X7             . A6=# CHARS IN FIND/LOC IMAGE    RN
)@@G@@@ @@@F          LXI,U     X1,1,X7   @ @@@F          L,U       X2,1,X4   RO
)@@G@@@ @@@F          L         A0,A6     @G@@@F          LMJ       X11,BMOVE RP
)@@G@@        . MOVE STRING TO FIND/LOC IMAGE   @E@@@F          S         A0,0RQ
)@@G@@,X4           . SAVE # OF CHARS     @E@@@F          SP1       0,X3      RR
)@@G@@        . SET FIND/LOCATE KEY @C@@@F          J         *READ           RS
)@@G@@  . EXIT    @G@@@FFINDCHK   L,U       X1,IMAGE          . COMPARE IMAGE RT
)@@G@@TO FIND IMAGE     @ @@@F          L,U       X2,FIMAGE @D@@@F          L RU
)@@G@@        X3,ASCII          . GET ASCII KEY @E@@@F          S,H1      X3,BRV
)@@G@@ASCII         . STORE FOR BYTESUB   @ @@@F          L         A0,NFIMAGERW
)@@G@@@ @@@F          LMJ       X11,BCOMP @E@@@F          JNZ       A0,*READ  RX
)@@G@@        . IF NO COMPARE, EXIT @E@@@F          SLJ       PIMAGE          RY
)@@G@@  . PRINT IMAGE FOUND   @D@@@F          SZ        FINDKEY           . CLRZ
)@@G@@EAR FIND KEY@F@@@F          J         READ+1            . READ NEXT USERSA
)@@G@@ COMMAND    @E@@@FLOCATE    L,U       X3,LOCKEY         . PT TO LOCATE DSB
)@@G@@ATA   @ @@@F          L,U       X4,NLIMAGE@E@@@F          J         FINDSC
)@@G@@C1            . SAME AS FIND LOGIC  @H@@@FLOCCHK    L,U       X1,IMAGE  SD
)@@G@@        . SEARCH FOR LOCATE IMAGE IN PRESENT    @C@@@F          L,U     SE
)@@G@@  X2,LIMAGE         .   IMAGE @E@@@F          L         A1,NIMAGE       SF
)@@G@@  . # OF WORDS IN IMAGE @D@@@F          L         A0,ASCII          . GESG
)@@G@@T ASCII KEY @E@@@F          S,H1      A0,BASCII         . STORE FOR BYTESH
)@@G@@SUB   @F@@@F          MSI       A1,FACT,A0        . CONVERT WORDS TO CHASI
)@@G@@RS    @ @@@F          L         A2,NLIMAGE@A@@@F          LMJ       X11,SJ
)@@G@@FINDFIELD   @D@@@F          J         *READ             . NO FIND, EXIT SK
)@@G@@@D@@@F          SLJ       PIMAGE            . PRINT IMAGE   @E@@@F      SL
)@@G@@    SZ        LOCKEY            . CLEAR LOCATE KEY    @F@@@F          J SM
)@@G@@        READ+1            . READ NEXT USER COMMAND    @G@@@FTOP       TNSN
)@@G@@Z       PARTBL+14         . IS THERE AN OUTPUT ELEMENT?     @G@@@F      SO
)@@G@@    J         TOPC              . NO, DON'T BOTHER WITH WARNING   @E@@@FSP
)@@G@@          TREAD$    MESS15,NMESS15 BUFF,EXIT . PRINT WARNING@F@@@F      SQ
)@@G@@    L         A0,('Y     ')     . IF USER ANSWERED 'Y',     @F@@@F      SR
)@@G@@    TE        A0,BUFF           .   INITIALIZE EVERYTHING   @F@@@F      SS
)@@G@@    J         READ+1            . OTHERWISE, IGNORE COMMAND @D@@@FTOPC  ST
)@@G@@    L,U       X1,NCOUNT-1       . CLEAR COUNTS  @ @@@F          SZ      SU
)@@G@@  COUNT,X1  @ @@@F          JGD       X1,$-1    @D@@@F          L,U     SV
)@@G@@  X1,NKEYS-1        . CLEAR KEYS    @ @@@F          SZ        KEYS,X1   SW
)@@G@@@ @@@F          JGD       X1,$-1    @E@@@F          PRINT$    MESS16,NMESX
)@@G@@SS16    . PRINT 'TOP' MESSAGE @E@@@F          J         INIT            SY
)@@G@@  . GO TO INITIALIZATION@A@@@FPRINT     L,U       X3,PRINTKEY     @F@@@FSZ
)@@G@@          SLJ       NINT              . PROCESS INTEGER FIELD     @C@@@FTA
)@@G@@          J         *READ             . RETURN  @ @@@FNEXT      L,U     TB
)@@G@@  X3,NEXTKEY@F@@@F          SLJ       NINT              . PROCESS INTEGETC
)@@G@@R FIELD     @C@@@F          J         *READ             . RETURN  @F@@@FTD
)@@G@@GO        L,U       X3,NEXTKEY        . PROCESS INTEGER FIELD     @H@@@FTE
)@@G@@          SLJ       NINT              .    USING SAME KEY AS NEXT COMMANTF
)@@G@@D     @I@@@F          L         A0,NEXTKEY        . CALC LINE NUMBER DIFTG
)@@G@@FERENCE FROM CURRENT    @ @@@F          AN        A0,LINENO @E@@@F      TH
)@@G@@    S         A0,NEXTKEY        . STORE AS NEXT KEY   @F@@@F          JPTI
)@@G@@        A0,*READ          . RETURN IF FORWARD IN FILE @G@@@F          PRTJ
)@@G@@INT$    MESS20,NMESS20    . IF BACKWARD, PRINT DIAGNOSTIC   @D@@@F      TK
)@@G@@    SZ        NEXTKEY           . CLEAR NEXT KEY@F@@@F          J       TL
)@@G@@  READ+1            . GET NEXT USER COMMAND     @E@@@FLINE      E$DIT   TM
)@@G@@  EPKT              . INITIALIZE EDITOR   @D@@@F          E$DECV    LINETN
)@@G@@NO            . LINE NUMBER   @C@@@F          E$PRINT                   TO
)@@G@@  . PRINT IT@F@@@F          J         READ+1            . GET NEXT USER TP
)@@G@@COMMAND     @H@@@F. ****************************************************TQ
)@@G@@**********************  @H@@@F. ******* PROCESS INTEGER FIELD SUBROUTINETR
)@@G@@                           *******  @H@@@F. ****************************TS
)@@G@@**********************************************  @^@@@FNINT      +       TT
)@@G@@  0   @E@@@F          SZ        0,X3              . CLEAR NEXT/PRINT KEYTU
)@@G@@@F@@@F          LXI,U     X1,1,X7           . IS THERE ANOTHER FIELD?   TV
)@@G@@@ @@@F          L         R1,CREAD  @A@@@F          LMJ       X11,GETFIETW
)@@G@@LD    @E@@@F          J         *NINT             . NO, JUST RETURN     TX
)@@G@@@F@@@F          LXI       X1,A1             . YES, CONVERT TO BINARY    TY
)@@G@@@ @@@F          LMJ       X11,BINT  @D@@@F          J         ERR5      TZ
)@@G@@        . SYNTAX ERROR  @G@@@F          AN,U      A2,1              . SEUA
)@@G@@T NEXT/PRINT KEY TO NUMBER-1  @E@@@F          JN        A2,ERR5         UB
)@@G@@  . NUMBER MUST BE > 0  @ @@@F          S         A2,0,X3   @C@@@F      UC
)@@G@@    J         *NINT             . RETURN  @H@@@E. **********************UD
)@@G@@****************************************************  @H@@@E. ******* PRUE
)@@G@@INT IMAGE SUBROUTINE                                     *******  @H@@@EUF
)@@G@@. **********************************************************************UG
)@@G@@****  @^@@@EPIMAGE    +         0   @D@@@E          TN        CONTROL   UH
)@@G@@        . CONTROL IMAGE?@B@@@E          J         PIMAGE1           . NOUI

)@@G@@****************************  @H@@@E. ******* OUTPUT IMAGE SUBROUTINE   UY
)@@G@@                                 *******  @H@@@E. **********************UZ
)@@G@@****************************************************  @^@@@EOUTPUT    + VA
)@@G@@        0   @G@F@E          L,U       X3,3              . UPDATE DATA ORVB

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF**[@@@@CTS@[=@ @@@@      SUBROUTINE SORTRF(RT,EP)*[@@@@CTS@[,YL
)@@G@@@^@@@@      PARAMETER LEN=5000*[@@@@CTS@[8@ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER (YM
)@@G@@A-Z)  *[@@@@CTS@]]@A@@@@      FD(I,K)=FLD(IABS(6*I-6),6,K)  *[@@@@CTS@]GYN

)@@G@@X(LEN),WORK(LEN),BUF(22),B(6),IC,IW *[@@@@CTS@])@B@@@@      IF (RT.GT.LEYP

)@@G@@N 2   *[@@@@CTS@]"@#@@@@      DO 10 I=1,RT*[@@@@CTS@#C@B@@@@   10 CALL BYS
)@@G@@UF2(5,A(I,1),6,LEN)  @ INPUT  *[@@@@CTS@#M@B@@@@C     CALL NTRAN(2,22,10YT

)@@G@@-RT,NDX,WORK,A(1,5))    *[@@@@CTS@^^@#@@@@      DO 15 I=1,RT*[@@@@CTS@^IYX

)@@G@@I=1,EP*[@@@@CTS@A=@#@@@@      J=NDX(I)    *[@@@@CTS@A,@^@@@@      LC=H1(ZI
)@@G@@A(J,7))     *[@@@@CTS@A8@C@@@@      ENCODE (25,BUF)A(J,5),A(J,6),LC,A(J,ZJ
)@@G@@8)    *[@@@@CTS@B]@B@@@@   25 FORMAT(1X,2A6,2X,O2,' (',O6,') (')  *[@@@@ZK
)@@G@@CTS@BG@#@@@@      CALL EPNAME *[@@@@CTS@BQ@^@@@@      GO TO (30,46),KGO ZL
)@@G@@*[@@@@CTS@B)@#@@@@   30 IRT=IRT+1   *[@@@@CTS@B%@ @@@@      IF (IRT.GT.RZM
)@@G@@T) GO TO 50 *[@@@@CTS@B4@A@@@@      CALL BUF2(5,B,6,1)    @ INPUT *[@@@@ZN
)@@G@@CTS@B"@C@@@@   46 IF (FD(1,A(J,5))-FD(1,B(5))) 45,26,30     *[@@@@CTS@CCZO
